Kuhulin: event game GunGame

Kuhulin: /event game - Select a event game (case sensitive) /event gamemode <normal/battlefield> - Toggles the 'Battlefield' setting for events /event spawnfile - Select a spawnfile for the event /event kit - Select a kit for the event /event open - Opens the event for players to join /event close - Closes the event from player entries /event start - Starts the event /event end - Ends the event /event cancel - Cancels the event (also cancels auto events) /event debug - Activate debug mode, useful for reporting errors
